ONE & TWO TECH DRIVE Tech Drive in Andover is a three-building Class A Office Park totaling over 330,000 square feet. Both One and Two Tech Drive have undergone significant lobby and common area make- overs, including a new cafe and fitness center located at Two Tech Drive. One and Two Tech Drive offer suites for tenants ranging from 3,000 square feet to 60,000 square feet. Andover Tech Drive’s unparalleled location at I-93 and River Road Interchange offers immediate access to I-495, while Route 128/I-95 is only a few minute’s drive to the south. Downtown Boston and Logan International Airport are only 30 minutes away. Area amenities include restaurants, hotels, fitness center and daycare. i roe : | gt eee /f\ we <a}  # =| ( Ld i \ a" a i im iP at I iP a <I =) i ~~ <P mentee a = 5 rR i Sa B We a Zz! w mm = Es raat " = ‘i es | mgd — iy ~~
